    30	/// The main datatype for rendering graphics.
    31	///
    32	/// A `Scene` stores a sequence of drawing commands, their context, and the
    33	/// associated resources, which can later be rendered.
    34	///
    35	/// Most users will render this using [`Renderer::render_to_texture`][crate::Renderer::render_to_texture].
    36	///
    37	/// Rendering from a `Scene` will *not* clear it, which should be done in a separate step, by calling [`Scene::reset`].
    38	///
    39	/// If this is not done for a scene which is retained (to avoid allocations) between frames, this will likely
    40	/// quickly increase the complexity of the render result, leading to crashes or potential host system instability.
    41	#[derive(Clone, Default)]
    42	pub struct Scene {
    43	    encoding: Encoding,
    44	    #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
    45	    estimator: vello_encoding::BumpEstimator,
    46	}
    47	static_assertions::assert_impl_all!(Scene: Send, Sync);
    48	
    49	impl Scene {
    50	    /// Creates a new scene.
    51	    pub fn new() -> Self {
    52	        Self::default()
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    /// Removes all content from the scene.
    56	    pub fn reset(&mut self) {
    57	        self.encoding.reset();
    58	        #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
    59	        self.estimator.reset();
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    /// Tally up the bump allocator estimate for the current state of the encoding,
    63	    /// taking into account an optional `transform` applied to the entire scene.
    64	    #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
    65	    pub fn bump_estimate(&self, transform: Option<Affine>) -> BumpAllocatorMemory {
    66	        self.estimator
    67	            .tally(transform.as_ref().map(Transform::from_kurbo).as_ref())
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    /// Returns the underlying raw encoding.
    71	    pub fn encoding(&self) -> &Encoding {
    72	        &self.encoding
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    /// Returns a mutable reference to the underlying raw encoding.
    76	    ///
    77	    /// This can be used to more easily create invalid scenes, and so should be used with care.
    78	    pub fn encoding_mut(&mut self) -> &mut Encoding {
    79	        &mut self.encoding
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    /// Pushes a new layer clipped by the specified shape and composed with
    83	    /// previous layers using the specified blend mode.
    84	    ///
    85	    /// Every drawing command after this call will be clipped by the shape
    86	    /// until the layer is popped.
    87	    ///
    88	    /// **However, the transforms are *not* saved or modified by the layer stack.**
    89	    ///
    90	    /// Clip layers (`blend` = [`Mix::Clip`]) should have an alpha value of 1.0.
    91	    /// For an opacity group with non-unity alpha, specify [`Mix::Normal`].
    92	    pub fn push_layer(
    93	        &mut self,
    94	        blend: impl Into<BlendMode>,
    95	        alpha: f32,
    96	        transform: Affine,
    97	        clip: &impl Shape,
    98	    ) {
    99	        let blend = blend.into();
   100	        if blend.mix == Mix::Clip && alpha != 1.0 {
   101	            log::warn!("Clip mix mode used with semitransparent alpha");
   102	        }
   103	        let t = Transform::from_kurbo(&transform);
   104	        self.encoding.encode_transform(t);
   105	        self.encoding.encode_fill_style(Fill::NonZero);
   106	        if !self.encoding.encode_shape(clip, true) {
   107	            // If the layer shape is invalid, encode a valid empty path. This suppresses
   108	            // all drawing until the layer is popped.
   109	            self.encoding.encode_empty_shape();
   110	            #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
   111	            {
   112	                use peniko::kurbo::PathEl;
   113	                let path = [PathEl::MoveTo(Point::ZERO), PathEl::LineTo(Point::ZERO)];
   114	                self.estimator.count_path(path.into_iter(), &t, None);
   115	            }
   116	        } else {
   117	            #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
   118	            self.estimator.count_path(clip.path_elements(0.1), &t, None);
   119	        }
   120	        self.encoding
   121	            .encode_begin_clip(blend, alpha.clamp(0.0, 1.0));
   122	    }
   123	
   124	    /// Pops the current layer.
   125	    pub fn pop_layer(&mut self) {
   126	        self.encoding.encode_end_clip();
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    /// Draw a rounded rectangle blurred with a gaussian filter.
   130	    pub fn draw_blurred_rounded_rect(
   131	        &mut self,
   132	        transform: Affine,
   133	        rect: Rect,
   134	        brush: Color,
   135	        radius: f64,
   136	        std_dev: f64,
   137	    ) {
   138	        // The impulse response of a gaussian filter is infinite.
   139	        // For performance reason we cut off the filter at some extent where the response is close to zero.
   140	        let kernel_size = 2.5 * std_dev;
   141	
   142	        let shape: Rect = rect.inflate(kernel_size, kernel_size);
   143	        self.draw_blurred_rounded_rect_in(&shape, transform, rect, brush, radius, std_dev);
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    /// Draw a rounded rectangle blurred with a gaussian filter in `shape`.
   147	    ///
   148	    /// For performance reasons, `shape` should not extend more than approximately 2.5 times
   149	    /// `std_dev` away from the edges of `rect` (as any such points will not be perceptably painted to,
   150	    /// but calculations will still be performed for them).
   151	    ///
   152	    /// This method effectively draws the blurred rounded rectangle clipped to the given shape.
   153	    /// If just the blurred rounded rectangle is desired without clipping,
   154	    /// use the simpler [`Self::draw_blurred_rounded_rect`].
   155	    /// For many users, that method will be easier to use.
   156	    pub fn draw_blurred_rounded_rect_in(
   157	        &mut self,
   158	        shape: &impl Shape,
   159	        transform: Affine,
   160	        rect: Rect,
   161	        brush: Color,
   162	        radius: f64,
   163	        std_dev: f64,
   164	    ) {
   165	        let t = Transform::from_kurbo(&transform);
   166	        self.encoding.encode_transform(t);
   167	
   168	        self.encoding.encode_fill_style(Fill::NonZero);
   169	        if self.encoding.encode_shape(&shape, true) {
   170	            let brush_transform =
   171	                Transform::from_kurbo(&transform.pre_translate(rect.center().to_vec2()));
   172	            if self.encoding.encode_transform(brush_transform) {
   173	                self.encoding.swap_last_path_tags();
   174	            }
   175	            self.encoding.encode_blurred_rounded_rect(
   176	                brush,
   177	                rect.width() as _,
   178	                rect.height() as _,
   179	                radius as _,
   180	                std_dev as _,
   181	            );
   182	        }
   183	    }
   184	
   185	    /// Fills a shape using the specified style and brush.
   186	    #[expect(
   187	        single_use_lifetimes,
   188	        reason = "False positive: https://github.com/rust-lang/rust/issues/129255"
   189	    )]
   190	    pub fn fill<'b>(
   191	        &mut self,
   192	        style: Fill,
   193	        transform: Affine,
   194	        brush: impl Into<BrushRef<'b>>,
   195	        brush_transform: Option<Affine>,
   196	        shape: &impl Shape,
   197	    ) {
   198	        let t = Transform::from_kurbo(&transform);
   199	        self.encoding.encode_transform(t);
   200	        self.encoding.encode_fill_style(style);
   201	        if self.encoding.encode_shape(shape, true) {
   202	            if let Some(brush_transform) = brush_transform {
   203	                if self
   204	                    .encoding
   205	                    .encode_transform(Transform::from_kurbo(&(transform * brush_transform)))
   206	                {
   207	                    self.encoding.swap_last_path_tags();
   208	                }
   209	            }
   210	            self.encoding.encode_brush(brush, 1.0);
   211	            #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
   212	            self.estimator
   213	                .count_path(shape.path_elements(0.1), &t, None);
   214	        }
   215	    }
   216	
   217	    /// Strokes a shape using the specified style and brush.
   218	    #[expect(
   219	        single_use_lifetimes,
   220	        reason = "False positive: https://github.com/rust-lang/rust/issues/129255"
   221	    )]
   222	    pub fn stroke<'b>(
   223	        &mut self,
   224	        style: &Stroke,
   225	        transform: Affine,
   226	        brush: impl Into<BrushRef<'b>>,
   227	        brush_transform: Option<Affine>,
   228	        shape: &impl Shape,
   229	    ) {
   230	        // The setting for tolerance are a compromise. For most applications,
   231	        // shape tolerance doesn't matter, as the input is likely Bézier paths,
   232	        // which is exact. Note that shape tolerance is hard-coded as 0.1 in
   233	        // the encoding crate.
   234	        //
   235	        // Stroke tolerance is a different matter. Generally, the cost scales
   236	        // with inverse O(n^6), so there is moderate rendering cost to setting
   237	        // too fine a value. On the other hand, error scales with the transform
   238	        // applied post-stroking, so may exceed visible threshold. When we do
   239	        // GPU-side stroking, the transform will be known. In the meantime,
   240	        // this is a compromise.
   241	        const SHAPE_TOLERANCE: f64 = 0.01;
   242	        const STROKE_TOLERANCE: f64 = SHAPE_TOLERANCE;
   243	
   244	        const GPU_STROKES: bool = true; // Set this to `true` to enable GPU-side stroking
   245	        if GPU_STROKES {
   246	            if style.width == 0. {
   247	                return;
   248	            }
   249	
   250	            let t = Transform::from_kurbo(&transform);
   251	            self.encoding.encode_transform(t);
   252	            let encoded_stroke = self.encoding.encode_stroke_style(style);
   253	            debug_assert!(encoded_stroke, "Stroke width is non-zero");
   254	
   255	            // We currently don't support dashing on the GPU. If the style has a dash pattern, then
   256	            // we convert it into stroked paths on the CPU and encode those as individual draw
   257	            // objects.
   258	            let encode_result = if style.dash_pattern.is_empty() {
   259	                #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
   260	                self.estimator
   261	                    .count_path(shape.path_elements(SHAPE_TOLERANCE), &t, Some(style));
   262	                self.encoding.encode_shape(shape, false)
   263	            } else {
   264	                // TODO: We currently collect the output of the dash iterator because
   265	                // `encode_path_elements` wants to consume the iterator. We want to avoid calling
   266	                // `dash` twice when `bump_estimate` is enabled because it internally allocates.
   267	                // Bump estimation will move to resolve time rather than scene construction time,
   268	                // so we can revert this back to not collecting when that happens.
   269	                let dashed = peniko::kurbo::dash(
   270	                    shape.path_elements(SHAPE_TOLERANCE),
   271	                    style.dash_offset,
   272	                    &style.dash_pattern,
   273	                )
   274	                .collect::<Vec<_>>();
   275	                #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
   276	                self.estimator
   277	                    .count_path(dashed.iter().copied(), &t, Some(style));
   278	                self.encoding
   279	                    .encode_path_elements(dashed.into_iter(), false)
   280	            };
   281	            if encode_result {
   282	                if let Some(brush_transform) = brush_transform {
   283	                    if self
   284	                        .encoding
   285	                        .encode_transform(Transform::from_kurbo(&(transform * brush_transform)))
   286	                    {
   287	                        self.encoding.swap_last_path_tags();
   288	                    }
   289	                }
   290	                self.encoding.encode_brush(brush, 1.0);
   291	            }
   292	        } else {
   293	            let stroked = peniko::kurbo::stroke(
   294	                shape.path_elements(SHAPE_TOLERANCE),
   295	                style,
   296	                &StrokeOpts::default(),
   297	                STROKE_TOLERANCE,
   298	            );
   299	            self.fill(Fill::NonZero, transform, brush, brush_transform, &stroked);
   300	        }
   301	    }
   302	
   303	    /// Draws an image at its natural size with the given transform.
   304	    pub fn draw_image(&mut self, image: &Image, transform: Affine) {
   305	        self.fill(
   306	            Fill::NonZero,
   307	            transform,
   308	            image,
   309	            None,
   310	            &Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, image.width as f64, image.height as f64),
   311	        );
   312	    }

   314	    /// Returns a builder for encoding a glyph run.
   315	    pub fn draw_glyphs(&mut self, font: &Font) -> DrawGlyphs<'_> {
   316	        // TODO: Integrate `BumpEstimator` with the glyph cache.

   319	
   320	    /// Appends a child scene.
   321	    ///
   322	    /// The given transform is applied to every transform in the child.
   323	    /// This is an O(N) operation.
   324	    pub fn append(&mut self, other: &Self, transform: Option<Affine>) {
   325	        let t = transform.as_ref().map(Transform::from_kurbo);
   326	        self.encoding.append(&other.encoding, &t);
   327	        #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
   328	        self.estimator.append(&other.estimator, t.as_ref());
   329	    }
   330	}

   332	impl From<Encoding> for Scene {
   333	    fn from(encoding: Encoding) -> Self {
   334	        // It's fine to create a default estimator here, and that field will be
   335	        // removed at some point - see https://github.com/linebender/vello/issues/541
   336	        Self {
   337	            encoding,
   338	            #[cfg(feature = "bump_estimate")]
   339	            estimator: vello_encoding::BumpEstimator::default(),
   340	        }
   341	    }
   342	}

   344	/// Builder for encoding a glyph run.
   345	///
   346	/// Created using [`Scene::draw_glyphs`].
   347	pub struct DrawGlyphs<'a> {
   348	    scene: &'a mut Scene,
   349	    run: GlyphRun,
   350	    brush: BrushRef<'a>,
   351	    brush_alpha: f32,
   352	}
   353	
   354	impl<'a> DrawGlyphs<'a> {
   355	    /// Creates a new builder for encoding a glyph run for the specified
   356	    /// encoding with the given font.
   357	    pub fn new(scene: &'a mut Scene, font: &Font) -> Self {
   358	        let coords_start = scene.encoding.resources.normalized_coords.len();
   359	        let glyphs_start = scene.encoding.resources.glyphs.len();
   360	        let stream_offsets = scene.encoding.stream_offsets();
   361	        Self {
   362	            scene,
   363	            run: GlyphRun {
   364	                font: font.clone(),
   365	                transform: Transform::IDENTITY,
   366	                glyph_transform: None,
   367	                font_size: 16.0,
   368	                hint: false,
   369	                normalized_coords: coords_start..coords_start,
   370	                style: Fill::NonZero.into(),
   371	                glyphs: glyphs_start..glyphs_start,
   372	                stream_offsets,
   373	            },
   374	            brush: palette::css::BLACK.into(),
   375	            brush_alpha: 1.0,
   376	        }
   377	    }
   378	
   379	    /// Sets the global transform. This is applied to all glyphs after the offset
   380	    /// translation.
   381	    ///
   382	    /// The default value is the identity matrix.
   383	    #[must_use]
   384	    pub fn transform(mut self, transform: Affine) -> Self {
   385	        self.run.transform = Transform::from_kurbo(&transform);
   386	        self
   387	    }
   388	
   389	    /// Sets the per-glyph transform. This is applied to all glyphs prior to
   390	    /// offset translation. This is common used for applying a shear to simulate
   391	    /// an oblique font.
   392	    ///
   393	    /// The default value is `None`.
   394	    #[must_use]
   395	    pub fn glyph_transform(mut self, transform: Option<Affine>) -> Self {
   396	        self.run.glyph_transform = transform.map(|xform| Transform::from_kurbo(&xform));
   397	        self
   398	    }

   402	    /// The default value is 16.0.

   407	    }

   241	    /// Push a new layer with the given properties.
   242	    ///
   243	    /// Note that the mask, if provided, needs to have the same size as the render context. Otherwise,
   244	    /// it will be ignored. In addition to that, the mask will not be affected by the current
   245	    /// transformation matrix in place.
   246	    pub fn push_layer(
   247	        &mut self,
   248	        clip_path: Option<&BezPath>,
   249	        blend_mode: Option<BlendMode>,
   250	        opacity: Option<f32>,
   251	        mask: Option<Mask>,
   252	    ) {
   253	        let mask = mask.and_then(|m| {
   254	            if m.width() != self.width || m.height() != self.height {
   255	                None
   256	            } else {
   257	                Some(m)
   258	            }
   259	        });
   260	
   261	        let blend_mode = blend_mode.unwrap_or(BlendMode::new(Mix::Normal, Compose::SrcOver));
   262	        let opacity = opacity.unwrap_or(1.0);
   263

   265	            clip_path,
   266	            self.fill_rule,
   267	            self.transform,
   268	            blend_mode,
   269	            opacity,
   270	            mask,
   271	        );
   272	    }

     1	// Copyright 2025 the Vello Authors
     2	// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 OR MIT
     3	
     4	use crate::RenderMode;
     5	use crate::dispatch::Dispatcher;
     6	use crate::fine::{F32Kernel, Fine, FineKernel, U8Kernel};
     7	use crate::kurbo::{Affine, BezPath, Stroke};
     8	use crate::peniko::{BlendMode, Fill};
     9	use crate::region::Regions;
    10	use crate::strip_generator::StripGenerator;
    11	use vello_common::coarse::Wide;
    12	use vello_common::encode::EncodedPaint;
    13	use vello_common::fearless_simd::{Fallback, Level, Simd};
    14	use vello_common::mask::Mask;
    15	use vello_common::paint::Paint;
    16	
    17	#[derive(Debug)]
    18	pub(crate) struct SingleThreadedDispatcher {
    19	    wide: Wide,
    20	    strip_generator: StripGenerator,
    21	    level: Level,
    22	}
    23	
    24	impl SingleThreadedDispatcher {
    25	    pub(crate) fn new(width: u16, height: u16, level: Level) -> Self {
    26	        let wide = Wide::new(width, height);
    27	        let strip_generator = StripGenerator::new(width, height, level);
    28	
    29	        Self {
    30	            wide,
    31	            strip_generator,
    32	            level,
    33	        }
    34	    }
    35	
    36	    fn rasterize_with<S: Simd, F: FineKernel<S>>(
    37	        &self,
    38	        simd: S,
    39	        buffer: &mut [u8],
    40	        width: u16,
    41	        height: u16,
    42	        encoded_paints: &[EncodedPaint],
    43	    ) {
    44	        let mut buffer = Regions::new(width, height, buffer);
    45	        let mut fine = Fine::<S, F>::new(simd);
    46	
    47	        buffer.update_regions(|region| {
    48	            let x = region.x;
    49	            let y = region.y;
    50	
    51	            let wtile = self.wide.get(x, y);
    52	            fine.set_coords(x, y);
    53	
    54	            fine.clear(wtile.bg);
    55	            for cmd in &wtile.cmds {
    56	                fine.run_cmd(cmd, self.strip_generator.alpha_buf(), encoded_paints);
    57	            }
    58	
    59	            fine.pack(region);
    60	        });
    61	    }
    62	}
    63	
    64	impl Dispatcher for SingleThreadedDispatcher {
    65	    fn wide(&self) -> &Wide {
    66	        &self.wide
    67	    }
    68	
    69	    fn fill_path(&mut self, path: &BezPath, fill_rule: Fill, transform: Affine, paint: Paint) {
    70	        let wide = &mut self.wide;
    71	
    72	        let func = |strips| wide.generate(strips, fill_rule, paint, 0);
    73	        self.strip_generator
    74	            .generate_filled_path(path, fill_rule, transform, func);
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    fn stroke_path(&mut self, path: &BezPath, stroke: &Stroke, transform: Affine, paint: Paint) {
    78	        let wide = &mut self.wide;
    79	
    80	        let func = |strips| wide.generate(strips, Fill::NonZero, paint, 0);
    81	        self.strip_generator
    82	            .generate_stroked_path(path, stroke, transform, func);
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    fn push_layer(
    86	        &mut self,
    87	        clip_path: Option<&BezPath>,
    88	        fill_rule: Fill,
    89	        clip_transform: Affine,
    90	        blend_mode: BlendMode,
    91	        opacity: f32,
    92	        mask: Option<Mask>,
    93	    ) {
    94	        let clip = if let Some(c) = clip_path {
    95	            // This variable will always be assigned to in the closure, but the compiler can't recognize that.
    96	            // So just assign a dummy value here.
    97	            let mut strip_buf = &[][..];
    98	
    99	            self.strip_generator
   100	                .generate_filled_path(c, fill_rule, clip_transform, |strips| strip_buf = strips);
   101	
   102	            Some((strip_buf, fill_rule))
   103	        } else {
   104	            None
   105	        };
   106	
   107	        self.wide.push_layer(clip, blend_mode, mask, opacity, 0);
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    fn pop_layer(&mut self) {
   111	        self.wide.pop_layer();
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    fn reset(&mut self) {
   115	        self.wide.reset();
   116	        self.strip_generator.reset();
   117	    }
   118	
   119	    fn flush(&mut self) {}
   120	
   121	    fn rasterize(
   122	        &self,
   123	        buffer: &mut [u8],
   124	        render_mode: RenderMode,
   125	        width: u16,
   126	        height: u16,
   127	        encoded_paints: &[EncodedPaint],
   128	    ) {
   129	        match render_mode {
   130	            RenderMode::OptimizeSpeed => match self.level {
   131	                #[cfg(all(feature = "std", target_arch = "aarch64"))]
   132	                Level::Neon(n) => {
   133	                    self.rasterize_with::<vello_common::fearless_simd::Neon, U8Kernel>(
   134	                        n,
   135	                        buffer,
   136	                        width,
   137	                        height,
   138	                        encoded_paints,
   139	                    );
   140	                }
   141	                #[cfg(all(target_arch = "wasm32", target_feature = "simd128"))]
   142	                Level::WasmSimd128(w) => {
   143	                    self.rasterize_with::<vello_common::fearless_simd::WasmSimd128, U8Kernel>(
   144	                        w,
   145	                        buffer,
   146	                        width,
   147	                        height,
   148	                        encoded_paints,
   149	                    );
   150	                }
   151	                _ => self.rasterize_with::<Fallback, U8Kernel>(
   152	                    Fallback::new(),
   153	                    buffer,
   154	                    width,
   155	                    height,
   156	                    encoded_paints,
   157	                ),
   158	            },
   159	            RenderMode::OptimizeQuality => match self.level {
   160	                #[cfg(all(feature = "std", target_arch = "aarch64"))]
   161	                Level::Neon(n) => {
   162	                    self.rasterize_with::<vello_common::fearless_simd::Neon, F32Kernel>(
   163	                        n,
   164	                        buffer,
   165	                        width,
   166	                        height,
   167	                        encoded_paints,
   168	                    );
   169	                }
   170	                #[cfg(all(target_arch = "wasm32", target_feature = "simd128"))]
   171	                Level::WasmSimd128(w) => {
   172	                    self.rasterize_with::<vello_common::fearless_simd::WasmSimd128, F32Kernel>(
   173	                        w,
   174	                        buffer,
   175	                        width,
   176	                        height,
   177	                        encoded_paints,
   178	                    );
   179	                }
   180	                _ => self.rasterize_with::<Fallback, F32Kernel>(
   181	                    Fallback::new(),
   182	                    buffer,
   183	                    width,
   184	                    height,
   185	                    encoded_paints,
   186	                ),
   187	            },
   188	        }
   189	    }
   190	}

    15	struct Layer {
    16	    /// Whether the layer has a clip associated with it.
    17	    clip: bool,
    18	    /// The blend mode with which this layer should be blended into
    19	    /// the previous layer.

    28	
    29	impl Layer {
    30	    /// Whether the layer actually requires allocating a new scratch buffer
    31	    /// for drawing its contents.
    32	    fn needs_buf(&self) -> bool {
    33	        self.blend_mode.mix != Mix::Normal
    34	            || self.blend_mode.compose != Compose::SrcOver
    35	            || self.opacity != 1.0
    36	            || self.mask.is_some()
    37	            || !self.clip
    38	    }
    39	}

   174	    /// Get the wide tile at a certain index.
   175	    ///
   176	    /// Panics if the index is out-of-range.
   177	    pub fn get(&self, x: u16, y: u16) -> &WideTile {
   178	        assert!(
   179	            x < self.width_tiles() && y < self.height_tiles(),
   180	            "attempted to access out-of-bounds wide tile"
   181	        );
   182

   184	    }

   325	    pub fn push_layer(
   326	        &mut self,
   327	        clip_path: Option<(impl Into<Box<[Strip]>>, Fill)>,
   328	        blend_mode: BlendMode,
   329	        mask: Option<Mask>,
   330	        opacity: f32,
   331	        thread_idx: u8,
   332	    ) {
   333	        // Some explanations about what is going on here: We support the concept of
   334	        // layers, where a user can push a new layer (with certain properties), draw some
   335	        // stuff, and finally pop the layer, as part of which the layer as a whole will be
   336	        // blended into the previous layer.
   337	        // There are 3 "straightforward" properties that can be set for each layer:
   338	        // 1) The blend mode that should be used to blend the layer into the backdrop.
   339	        // 2) A mask that will be applied to the whole layer in the very end before blending.
   340	        // 3) An optional opacity that will be applied to the whole layer before blending (this
   341	        //    could in theory be simulated with an alpha mask, but since it's a common operation and
   342	        //    we only have a single opacity, this can easily be optimized.
   343	        //
   344	        // Finally, you can also add a clip path to the layer. However, clipping has its own
   345	        // more complicated logic for pushing/popping buffers where drawing is also suppressed
   346	        // in clipped-out wide tiles. Because of this, in case we have one of the above properties
   347	        // AND a clipping path, we will actually end up pushing two buffers, the first one handles
   348	        // the three properties and the second one is just for clip paths. That is a bit wasteful
   349	        // and I believe it should be possible to process them all in just one go, but for now
   350	        // this is good enough, and it allows us to implement blending without too deep changes to
   351	        // the original clipping implementation.
   352	
   353	        let layer = Layer {
   354	            clip: clip_path.is_some(),
   355	            blend_mode,
   356	            opacity,
   357	            mask,
   358	        };
   359	
   360	        let needs_buf = layer.needs_buf();
   361	
   362	        // In case we do blending, masking or opacity, push one buffer per wide tile.
   363	        if needs_buf {
   364	            for x in 0..self.width_tiles() {
   365	                for y in 0..self.height_tiles() {
   366	                    self.get_mut(x, y).push_buf();
   367	                }
   368	            }
   369	        }
   370	
   371	        // If we have a clip path, push another buffer in the affected wide tiles.
   372	        // Note that it is important that we FIRST push the buffer for blending etc. and
   373	        // only then for clipping, otherwise we will use the empty clip buffer as the backdrop
   374	        // for blending!
   375	        if let Some((clip, fill)) = clip_path {
   376	            self.push_clip(clip, fill, thread_idx);
   377	        }
   378	
   379	        self.layer_stack.push(layer);
   380	    }
   381	
   382	    /// Pop a previously pushed layer.
   383	    pub fn pop_layer(&mut self) {
   384	        // This method basically unwinds everything we did in `push_layer`.
   385	
   386	        let layer = self.layer_stack.pop().unwrap();
   387	
   388	        if layer.clip {
   389	            self.pop_clip();
   390	        }
   391	
   392	        let needs_buf = layer.needs_buf();
   393	
   394	        if needs_buf {
   395	            for x in 0..self.width_tiles() {
   396	                for y in 0..self.height_tiles() {
   397	                    let t = self.get_mut(x, y);
   398	
   399	                    if let Some(mask) = layer.mask.clone() {
   400	                        t.mask(mask);

   550	    /// # Algorithm overview:
   551	    /// 1. Retrieve the top clip from the stack
   552	    /// 2. For each wide tile in the clip's bounding box:
   553	    ///    - If covered by zero winding: `pop_zero_clip`
   554	    ///    - If fully covered by non-zero winding: do nothing (was no-op)
   555	    ///    - If partially covered: render the clip and `pop_clip`
   556	    ///
   557	    /// This operation must be symmetric with `push_clip` to maintain a balanced clip stack.
   558	    fn pop_clip(&mut self) {
   559	        let Clip {
   560	            clip_bbox,
   561	            strips,
   562	            fill_rule,
   563	            #[cfg(feature = "multithreading")]
   564	            thread_idx,
   565	        } = self.clip_stack.pop().unwrap();
   566	        let n_strips = strips.len();
   567	
   568	        let mut cur_wtile_x = clip_bbox.x0();
   569	        let mut cur_wtile_y = clip_bbox.y0();
   570	        let mut pop_pending = false;
   571	
   572	        // Process each strip to determine the clipping state for each tile
   573	        for i in 0..n_strips.saturating_sub(1) {
   574	            let strip = &strips[i];
   575	            let strip_y = strip.strip_y();
   576	
   577	            // Skip strips before current tile row
   578	            if strip_y < cur_wtile_y {
   579	                continue;
   580	            }
   581	
   582	            // Process tiles in rows before this strip's row
   583	            // These tiles all had zero-winding clips
   584	            while cur_wtile_y < strip_y.min(clip_bbox.y1()) {
   585	                // Handle any pending clip pop from previous iteration
   586	                if core::mem::take(&mut pop_pending) {
   587	                    self.get_mut(cur_wtile_x, cur_wtile_y).pop_clip();
   588	                    cur_wtile_x += 1;
   589	                }
   590	
   591	                // Pop zero clips for all remaining tiles in this row
   592	                for wtile_x in cur_wtile_x..clip_bbox.x1() {
   593	                    self.get_mut(wtile_x, cur_wtile_y).pop_zero_clip();
   594	                }
   595	                cur_wtile_x = clip_bbox.x0();
   596	                cur_wtile_y += 1;
   597	            }
   598	
   599	            // If we've reached the bottom of the clip bounding box, stop processing
   600	            if cur_wtile_y == clip_bbox.y1() {

   315	    pub(crate) fn run_cmd(&mut self, cmd: &Cmd, alphas: &[u8], paints: &[EncodedPaint]) {
   316	        match cmd {
   317	            Cmd::Fill(f) => {
   318	                self.fill(
   319	                    usize::from(f.x),
   320	                    usize::from(f.width),
   321	                    &f.paint,
   322	                    f.blend_mode
   323	                        .unwrap_or(BlendMode::new(Mix::Normal, Compose::SrcOver)),
   324	                    paints,
   325	                    None,
   326	                );
   327	            }
   328	            Cmd::AlphaFill(s) => {
   329	                self.fill(
   330	                    usize::from(s.x),
   331	                    usize::from(s.width),
   332	                    &s.paint,
   333	                    s.blend_mode
   334	                        .unwrap_or(BlendMode::new(Mix::Normal, Compose::SrcOver)),
   335	                    paints,
   336	                    Some(&alphas[s.alpha_idx..]),
   337	                );
   338	            }
   339	            Cmd::PushBuf => {
   340	                self.blend_buf.push([T::Numeric::ZERO; SCRATCH_BUF_SIZE]);
   341	            }
   342	            Cmd::PopBuf => {
   343	                self.blend_buf.pop();
   344	            }
   345	            Cmd::ClipFill(cf) => {
   346	                self.clip(cf.x as usize, cf.width as usize, None);
   347	            }
   348	            Cmd::ClipStrip(cs) => {
   349	                self.clip(
   350	                    cs.x as usize,
   351	                    cs.width as usize,
   352	                    Some(&alphas[cs.alpha_idx..]),
   353	                );
   354	            }
   355	            Cmd::Blend(b) => self.blend(*b),
   356	            Cmd::Mask(m) => {
   357	                let start_x = self.wide_coords.0 * WideTile::WIDTH;
   358	                let start_y = self.wide_coords.1 * Tile::HEIGHT;
   359	
   360	                let blend_buf = self.blend_buf.last_mut().unwrap();

   362	                let width = (blend_buf.len() / (Tile::HEIGHT as usize * COLOR_COMPONENTS)) as u16;
   363	                let y = start_y as u32 + u32x4::from_slice(self.simd, &[0, 1, 2, 3]);
   364	
   365	                let iter = (start_x..(start_x + width)).map(|x| {
   366	                    let x_in_range = x < m.width();
   367	
   368	                    macro_rules! sample {
   369	                        ($idx:expr) => {
   370	                            if x_in_range && (y[$idx] as u16) < m.height() {
   371	                                m.sample(x, y[$idx] as u16)
   372	                            } else {
   373	                                0
   374	                            }
   375	                        };
   376	                    }
   377	
   378	                    let s1 = sample!(0);
   379	                    let s2 = sample!(1);
   380	                    let s3 = sample!(2);
   381	                    let s4 = sample!(3);
   382	
   383	                    let samples = u8x16::from_slice(
   384	                        self.simd,
   385	                        &[
   386	                            s1, s1, s1, s1, s2, s2, s2, s2, s3, s3, s3, s3, s4, s4, s4, s4,
   387	                        ],
   388	                    );
   389	                    T::NumericVec::from_u8(self.simd, samples)
   390	                });
   391	
   392	                T::apply_mask(self.simd, blend_buf, iter);
   393	            }
   394	            Cmd::Opacity(o) => {
   395	                if *o != 1.0 {

   397

     4	//! Tests for clipping.

    19	#[vello_test(height = 8)]
    20	fn clip_single_wide_tile(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {
    21	    const WIDTH: f64 = 100.0;
    22	    assert!(WIDTH <= WideTile::WIDTH as f64, "Width larger than a tile");
    23	    const HEIGHT: f64 = Tile::HEIGHT as f64;
    24	    const OFFSET: f64 = WIDTH / 3.0;
    25	
    26	    let colors = [RED, GREEN, BLUE];
    27	
    28	    for (i, color) in colors.iter().enumerate() {
    29	        let clip_rect = Rect::new((i as f64) * OFFSET, 0.0, WIDTH, HEIGHT);
    30	        ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_rect.to_path(0.1));
    31	        ctx.set_paint(*color);
    32	        ctx.fill_rect(&Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, WIDTH, HEIGHT));
    33	    }
    34	    for _ in colors.iter() {
    35	        ctx.pop_layer();
    36	    }
    37	}

    40	fn clip_triangle_with_star(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {

    42	    triangle_path.move_to((10.0, 10.0));

    52	    let star_path = circular_star(Point::new(50., 50.), 13, 25., 45.);
    53	
    54	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&star_path);
    55	    ctx.set_paint(REBECCA_PURPLE);
    56	    ctx.fill_path(&triangle_path);
    57	    ctx.pop_layer();
    58	}

    60	#[vello_test]
    61	fn clip_rectangle_with_star_nonzero(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {
    62	    let rect = Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
    63	    // Create a self-intersecting star shape that will show the difference between fill rules
    64	    let star_path = crossed_line_star();
    65	
    66	    // Set the fill rule to NonZero before applying the clip
    67	    ctx.set_fill_rule(Fill::NonZero);
    68	    // Apply the star as a clip
    69	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&star_path);
    70	    // Draw a rectangle that should be clipped by the star
    71	    // The NonZero fill rule will treat self-intersecting regions as filled
    72	    ctx.set_paint(REBECCA_PURPLE);
    73	    ctx.fill_rect(&rect);
    74	    ctx.pop_layer();
    75	}

    77	#[vello_test]
    78	fn clip_rectangle_with_star_evenodd(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {
    79	    let rect = Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
    80	    // Create a self-intersecting star shape that will show the difference between fill rules
    81	    let star_path = crossed_line_star();
    82	
    83	    // Set the fill rule to EvenOdd before applying the clip
    84	    ctx.set_fill_rule(Fill::EvenOdd);
    85	    // Apply the star as a clip
    86	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&star_path);
    87	    // Draw a rectangle that should be clipped by the star
    88	    // The EvenOdd rule should create a "hole" in the middle where the paths overlap
    89	    ctx.set_paint(REBECCA_PURPLE);
    90	    ctx.fill_rect(&rect);
    91	    ctx.pop_layer();
    92	}

    94	#[vello_test(cpu_u8_tolerance = 1)]
    95	fn clip_deeply_nested_circles(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {
    96	    const INITIAL_RADIUS: f64 = 48.0;
    97	    const RADIUS_DECREMENT: f64 = 2.5;
    98	    const INNER_COUNT: usize = 10;
    99	    // `.ceil()` is not constant-evaluatable, so we have to do this at runtime.
   100	    let outer_count: usize =
   101	        (INITIAL_RADIUS / RADIUS_DECREMENT / INNER_COUNT as f64).ceil() as usize;
   102	    const COLORS: [Color; INNER_COUNT] = [
   103	        RED,
   104	        DARK_BLUE,
   105	        DARK_GREEN,
   106	        REBECCA_PURPLE,
   107	        BLACK,
   108	        BLUE,
   109	        GREEN,
   110	        RED,
   111	        DARK_BLUE,
   112	        DARK_GREEN,
   113	    ];
   114	
   115	    const COVER_RECT: Rect = Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
   116	    const CENTER: Point = Point::new(50.0, 50.0);
   117	    let mut radius = INITIAL_RADIUS;
   118	
   119	    for _ in 0..outer_count {
   120	        for color in COLORS.iter() {
   121	            let clip_circle = Circle::new(CENTER, radius).to_path(0.1);
   122	            draw_clipping_outline(ctx, &clip_circle);
   123	            ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_circle);
   124	
   125	            ctx.set_paint(*color);
   126	            ctx.fill_rect(&COVER_RECT);
   127	
   128	            radius -= RADIUS_DECREMENT;
   129	        }
   130	    }
   131	    for _ in 0..outer_count {
   132	        for _ in COLORS.iter() {
   133	            ctx.pop_layer();
   134	        }
   135	    }
   136	}
   137	
   138	#[vello_test(cpu_u8_tolerance = 1)]
   139	fn clip_rectangle_and_circle(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {
   140	    // Create first clipping region - a rectangle on the left side
   141	    let clip_rect = Rect::new(10.0, 30.0, 50.0, 70.0);
   142	
   143	    // Create second clipping region - a circle on the right side
   144	    let circle_center = Point::new(65.0, 50.0);
   145	    let circle_radius = 30.0;
   146	    let clip_circle = Circle::new(circle_center, circle_radius).to_path(0.1);
   147	
   148	    // Draw outlines of our clipping regions to visualize them
   149	    let stroke = Stroke::new(1.0);
   150	    ctx.set_paint(DARK_BLUE);
   151	    ctx.set_stroke(stroke);
   152	    ctx.stroke_rect(&clip_rect);
   153	    ctx.stroke_path(&clip_circle);
   154	
   155	    // Apply both clips
   156	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_rect.to_path(0.1));
   157	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_circle);
   158	
   159	    // Then a filled rectangle that covers most of the canvas
   160	    let large_rect = Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
   161	    ctx.set_paint(REBECCA_PURPLE);
   162	    ctx.fill_rect(&large_rect);
   163	    ctx.pop_layer();
   164	    ctx.pop_layer();
   165	}

   167	#[vello_test]
   168	fn clip_with_translation(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {
   169	    // Apply a translation transform
   170	    ctx.set_transform(Affine::translate((30.0, 30.0)));
   171	
   172	    // Create and apply a clipping rectangle
   173	    let clip_rect = Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 40.0, 40.0);
   174	    draw_clipping_outline(ctx, &clip_rect.to_path(0.1));
   175	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_rect.to_path(0.1));
   176	
   177	    // Draw a rectangle that should be clipped
   178	    let rect = Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
   179	    ctx.set_paint(REBECCA_PURPLE);
   180	    ctx.fill_rect(&rect);
   181	    ctx.pop_layer();
   182	}

   239	#[vello_test]
   240	fn clip_with_multiple_transforms(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {
   241	    // Apply initial transform
   242	    ctx.set_transform(Affine::rotate_about(
   243	        45.0 * PI / 180.0,
   244	        Point::new(50.0, 50.0),
   245	    ));
   246	
   247	    // Create and apply first clip
   248	    let clip_rect1 = Rect::new(20.0, 20.0, 80.0, 80.0);
   249	    draw_clipping_outline(ctx, &clip_rect1.to_path(0.1));
   250	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_rect1.to_path(0.1));
   251	
   252	    // Apply another transform
   253	    ctx.set_transform(Affine::scale(1.5));
   254	
   255	    // Create and apply second clip
   256	    let clip_rect2 = Rect::new(30.0, 30.0, 70.0, 70.0);
   257	    draw_clipping_outline(ctx, &clip_rect2.to_path(0.1));
   258	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_rect2.to_path(0.1));
   259	
   260	    // Draw a rectangle that should be clipped by both regions
   261	    let rect = Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
   262	    ctx.set_paint(REBECCA_PURPLE);
   263	    ctx.fill_rect(&rect);
   264	    ctx.pop_layer();
   265	    ctx.pop_layer();
   266	}

   268	#[vello_test(hybrid_tolerance = 1)]
   269	fn clip_with_save_restore(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {
   270	    // Create first clipping region - a rectangle on the left side
   271	    let clip_rect1 = Rect::new(10.0, 30.0, 50.0, 70.0);
   272	    draw_clipping_outline(ctx, &clip_rect1.to_path(0.1));
   273	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_rect1.to_path(0.1));
   274	
   275	    // Add second clipping region - a circle on the right side
   276	    let circle_center = Point::new(65.0, 50.0);
   277	    let circle_radius = 30.0;
   278	    let clip_circle = Circle::new(circle_center, circle_radius).to_path(0.1);
   279	    draw_clipping_outline(ctx, &clip_circle);
   280	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_circle);
   281	
   282	    // Draw a rectangle that should be clipped by both regions
   283	    let rect = Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
   284	    ctx.set_paint(REBECCA_PURPLE);
   285	    ctx.fill_rect(&rect);
   286	
   287	    // Restore to state before second clip
   288	    ctx.pop_layer();
   289	
   290	    // Draw another rectangle that should only be clipped by the first region
   291	    let rect2 = Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
   292	    ctx.set_paint(DARK_GREEN.with_alpha(0.5));
   293	    ctx.fill_rect(&rect2);
   294	    ctx.pop_layer();
   295	}

   298	fn clip_with_opacity(ctx: &mut impl Renderer) {
   299	    // Main body of the shape should be RGB 128, 128, 128. Anti-aliased part should be
   300	    // 191, 191, 191.
   301	    let clip_rect = Rect::new(10.5, 10.5, 89.5, 89.5);
   302	    ctx.push_clip_layer(&clip_rect.to_path(0.1));
   303	    ctx.set_paint(BLACK.with_alpha(0.5));
   304	    ctx.fill_rect(&Rect::new(0.0, 0.0, 100.0, 100.0));
   305	    ctx.pop_layer();
   306	}

   308	fn draw_clipping_outline(ctx: &mut impl Renderer, path: &BezPath) {
   309	    let stroke = Stroke::new(1.0);
   310	    ctx.set_paint(DARK_BLUE);
   311	    ctx.set_stroke(stroke);
   312	    ctx.stroke_path(path);
   313	}

   488	                let is_inside = match fill_rule {
   489	                    Fill::NonZero => strip.winding != 0,
   490	                    Fill::EvenOdd => strip.winding % 2 != 0,
   491	                };
   492	                if !is_inside {
   493	                    for wtile_x in cur_wtile_x..wtile_x_clamped {
   494	                        self.get_mut(wtile_x, cur_wtile_y).push_zero_clip();
   495	                    }
   496	                }
   497	                // If winding is nonzero, then wide tiles covered entirely
   498	                // by sparse fill are no-op (no clipping is applied).
   499	                cur_wtile_x = wtile_x_clamped;
   500	            }
   501	
   502	            // Process wide tiles covered by the strip - these need actual clipping
   503	            let next_strip = &strips[i + 1];
   504	            let width = ((next_strip.alpha_idx - strip.alpha_idx) / u32::from(Tile::HEIGHT)) as u16;
   505	            let wtile_x1 = (x + width).div_ceil(WideTile::WIDTH).min(clip_bbox.x1());
   506	            if cur_wtile_x < wtile_x1 {
   507	                for wtile_x in cur_wtile_x..wtile_x1 {
   508	                    self.get_mut(wtile_x, cur_wtile_y).push_clip();
   509	                }
   510	                cur_wtile_x = wtile_x1;
   511	            }
   512	        }
   513	
   514	        // Process any remaining wide tiles in the bounding box (all zero-winding)
   515	        while cur_wtile_y < clip_bbox.y1() {
   516	            for wtile_x in cur_wtile_x..clip_bbox.x1() {
   517	                self.get_mut(wtile_x, cur_wtile_y).push_zero_clip();
   518	            }
   519	            cur_wtile_x = clip_bbox.x0();
   520	            cur_wtile_y += 1;
   521	        }
   522	
   523	        // Prevent unused warning.
   524	        let _ = thread_idx;
   525	
   526	        self.clip_stack.push(Clip {
   527	            clip_bbox,
   528	            strips,
   529	            fill_rule,
   530	            #[cfg(feature = "multithreading")]
   531	            thread_idx,
   532	        });
   533	    }
   534	
   535	    /// Get the bounding box of the current clip region or the entire viewport if no clip regions are active.
   536	    fn get_bbox(&self) -> Bbox {
   537	        if let Some(top) = self.clip_stack.last() {
   538	            top.clip_bbox.clone()
   539	        } else {
   540	            // Convert pixel dimensions to wide tile coordinates
   541	            Bbox::new([0, 0, self.width_tiles(), self.height_tiles()])
   542	        }
   543	    }
   544	
   545	    /// Removes the most recently added clip region.
   546	    ///
   547	    /// This is the inverse operation of `push_clip`, carefully undoing all the clipping
   548	    /// operations while also handling any rendering needed for the clip region itself.
   549	    ///
   550	    /// # Algorithm overview:

   423	        let strips = strips.into();
   424	        let n_strips = strips.len();
   425	
   426	        // Calculate the bounding box of the clip path in strip coordinates
   427	        let path_bbox = if n_strips <= 1 {
   428	            Bbox::empty()
   429	        } else {
   430	            // Calculate the y range from first to last strip in wide tile coordinates
   431	            let wtile_y0 = strips[0].strip_y();
   432	            let wtile_y1 = strips[n_strips.saturating_sub(1)].strip_y() + 1;
   433

   435	            let mut wtile_x0 = strips[0].x / WideTile::WIDTH;
   436	            let mut wtile_x1 = wtile_x0;

   438	                let strip = &strips[i];

   445	            }
